  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_4e58f49b-c2e5-45e1-bd9d-a9da75d62b14'
      });

<span id="freeTextContainer15936051076290923240">Ella and Micha have been best friends since they were kids.   <span id="freeText15936051076290923240" style="display:none">Ella and Micha have been best friends since they were kids. But one tragic night shatters their friendship and their lives forever.<br /><br />Ella used to be a rule-breaker with fiery attitude who wore her heart on her sleeve. But she left everything behind when she went to college and transformed into someone that follows the rules, keeps everything together, and hides all her problems. But now it's summer break and she has nowhere else to go but home. <br /><br />Ella fears everything she worked so hard to bury might resurface, especially with Micha living right next door. If Micha tries to tempt the old her back, she knows that it will be hard to resist.<br /><br />Micha is sexy, smart, confident, and can get under Ella’s skin like no one else can. He knows everything about her, including her darkest secrets. And he’s determined to bring his best friend, and the girl he loves back, no matter what it takes. <br /><br />(New Adult Contemporary)<br />*Mature Content** Recommended for ages 17+ due to sexual situations and language.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer559862934" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1500804098089249556"><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/star.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>So I’m goin’ to go on the record and say that I didn’t give Jessica Sorensen five stars for this book.<br/><br/><b>She took them from me.</b><br/><br/>She took them from me with her absurdly beautiful story, with her heart-arresting characters, and with her words that belong in a jewelry box somewhere. <br/><br/>This author is <b>fucking</b> kickass.<br/><br/>And that’s all there is to say, really.<br/><br/>_____________________________________<br/><br/><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/title.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>They grew up together, you know.<br/><br/>Ella and Micha, I mean.<br/><br/>With nothing but a fence that begged to be jumped ove</span>
  <span id="freeText1500804098089249556" style="display:none"><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/star.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413203i/813262.jpg" alt=" photo star.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So I’m goin’ to go on the record and say that I didn’t give Jessica Sorensen five stars for this book.<br><br><b>She took them from me.</b><br><br>She took them from me with her absurdly beautiful story, with her heart-arresting characters, and with her words that belong in a jewelry box somewhere. <br><br>This author is <b>fucking</b> kickass.<br><br>And that’s all there is to say, really.<br><br>_____________________________________<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/title.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413203i/813263.jpg" alt=" photo title.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><br>They grew up together, you know.<br><br>Ella and Micha, I mean.<br><br>With nothing but a fence that begged to be jumped over between their two houses, these two were inseparable.<br><br>She was a wild child, and he was the boy with the wild smile.<br><br>Then suddenly jean-clad races against childhood turned into car races against asphalt.<br>Secrets whispered into ears became confessions whispered into each other’s mouths.<br>Bedroom windows were left open and front doors became locked.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/download6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413203i/813264._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo download6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And in one night, life became very cruel for one of them.<br><br>And Ella left.<br><br>♦ <b>
  <i> The girl he thinks he loves needs to disappear. </i>
</b> ♦<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/download7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413203i/813265._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo download7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>She wanted a new start and a new life and a new personality.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_mkejas7J0n1qaobbko1_500.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413203i/813266.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_mkejas7J0n1qaobbko1_500.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>♦ She put away her spit-fire honesty and learned the art of white lies.<br>♦ She washed off her thick eyeliner and bought pretty pink eyeshadow.<br>♦ She replaced her combat boots with ballet flats.<br>♦ She traded in her quick laughter for slow smiles.<br><br>Until she had to go back eight months later, that is. Back to her hometown where she left her best friend in the middle of the night.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/stargrove.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413203i/813267.png" alt=" photo stargrove.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> A long time ago, it felt like home, back when street racing and running wild felt natural, but now I just feel lost. </i>
</b><br><br>In what seems like minute-long hours… Ella is slammed back into a life she’d give anything to erase.<br><br>Well, almost everything.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_mn7huxHPaQ1r1y0g8o1_500.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413203i/813268._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_mn7huxHPaQ1r1y0g8o1_500.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>He is my best friend, my soul mate. In a perfect world, full of roses and sunshine we’d be together, but this world is full of broken homes, drunken fathers, and mothers who give up easily.</i>
</b><br><br>The only thing worse than leaving Micha… is falling in love with Micha.<br><br>And Ella did. <i>Hard</i>.<br><br>So when she finds herself face-to-face with her childhood best friend and the love of her life, she soon realizes a couple of things:<br><br>♥ He still sucks on his lower lip ring when he concentrates.<br>♥ He’s still the boy all the girls want to have at 2 a.m.<br>♥ He’s still the most mischievously beautiful boy Ella’s ever met.<br><br>And he remembers everything. <br><br>Not only is he not cashing in on Ella’s new act and the fact that she’s pretending not to even care for him, he’s going to do everything to bring back that girl he used to know. And he <i>will</i> fight dirty.<br><br><i>
  <b> I trap her down by the hips and conform her backside onto my lap. We fit together so perfectly it’s mind blowing and all those feelings I felt for her before she left come rushing back to me. I need more of her. Now. Oblivious to everyone around us, my hands gradually slide up her thighs.<br><br>“Micha.” She protests with a quiver in her voice. “Don’t. There are people…”<br><br>I silence her as my fingers brush the edges of her skirt. </b>
</i><br><br>But despite Micha’s wicked hands and heart-melting intentions…<br><br>Ella still tries to repaint the lines of their boundaries<br><br>Because all she wants is complete control over her life. And she wants to forget the night she lost all of it.<br><br><b>
  <i> It clicks and I push the door open.<br><br>The scream that leaves my mouth could shatter the world’s happiness into a thousand pieces. But the silence that follows it is enough to dissolve it completely. </i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_mfx0uePUgN1rmyw7yo1_500.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2478917344" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5087651700203247535"><b>YA Goodness!!</b><br/><br/>This is the first full-length book of the Ella and Micha saga. I enjoyed the novella so much and totally fell in love with these two love birds. I am enjoying taking their journey with them. <br/><br/>Childhood best friends, Micha fell in love with her at age fifteen and has been waiting three years for Ella to catch up.<br/><br/> <b>
  <i>She challenges me, pushes me, and pisses me off, but I wouldn’t have it any other way.</i>
</b><br/><br/>I don’t want to give any of the storyline away, but suffice it to say, this one kept</span>
  <span id="freeText5087651700203247535" style="display:none"><b>YA Goodness!!</b><br /><br />This is the first full-length book of the Ella and Micha saga. I enjoyed the novella so much and totally fell in love with these two love birds. I am enjoying taking their journey with them. <br /><br />Childhood best friends, Micha fell in love with her at age fifteen and has been waiting three years for Ella to catch up.<br /><br /> <b>
  <i>She challenges me, pushes me, and pisses me off, but I wouldn’t have it any other way.</i>
</b><br /><br />I don’t want to give any of the storyline away, but suffice it to say, this one kept me churning through the pages. It ends not so much on a cliff hanger, but there is more to come as their romantic relationship is just getting started. <br /><br />Talk about a s.l.o.w. b.u.r.n., but worth the wait. I am anticipating trouble ahead for this couple, so I am excited to read the next installment! <br /><br />I love tension and angst in my romance reads ;)</span>

<div id="review_457285060" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/457285060" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/457285060?book_show_action=true">Nov 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=young-adult-fiction">young-adult-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer457285060" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3513848921222573662"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"It was one of the things that made me fall in love with her; the fire, passion, and the need to stick up for the outcasts, even if it meant being an outcast herself."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397848ra/768095.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p><br/><br/>When Ella ran a away from home eigth months ago, she ran away because she wanted to forget. Forget about the past and everything that happened in the town she grew up in. But when she returns home from college, the walls she tried to built up around her heart slowly begin to fall apart when she's reunited with her b</span>
  <span id="freeText3513848921222573662" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"It was one of the things that made me fall in love with her; the fire, passion, and the need to stick up for the outcasts, even if it meant being an outcast herself."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397848ra/768095.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br>When Ella ran a away from home eigth months ago, she ran away because she wanted to forget. Forget about the past and everything that happened in the town she grew up in. But when she returns home from college, the walls she tried to built up around her heart slowly begin to fall apart when she's reunited with her best friend Micha. Ella and Micha have been next door neighbors almost their entire life and they have been inseperable ever since they were little. So, when Ella returns home as a new person, Micha is determined to bring the old Ella, the one he fell in love with, back. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Micha, this is who I have to be otherwise I can't breathe. Please just leave it alone. That dame fire might exist, but I want it gone." I spin my back to him, praying he'll listen to me for once, because if he keeps it up, sooner or later I won't be able to resist. <br>But Micha has never backed down on a challenge in his life.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>And so, Micha slowly but surely tries to win Ella back and he tries to make her realise that <i>"You can't just change who you are on the outside and expect it to change who you are on the inside"</i>...<br><br>To Micha there has never been anyone else. Sure, he's had his share of flings and hook-ups, but no other girl has ever been able to make him feel the way Ella does.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"As carefully as I can, I step over her bed and crawl in with Ella. I press my chest against her back, drape my arm over her waist, and feel the rhythm of her breathing. God, I've missed this way too much. It's not healthy. I burrow my face in her neck, smelling the scent of her hair, vanilla mixed with something that's only her. <br>I shut my eyes and for the first time in eight months, I fall into a peaceful sleep."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>As a musician Micha also expresses his feelings towards Ella in the beautiful lyrics of the song he dedicated to her:<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>" I see it in your beautiful eyes, like a spot on the sun.<br>The things you want to hide, buried deep inside you.<br>Blinded by your light.<br>It almost hurts to look at, almost hurts to breathe.<br>Never can you look at the things no one ever sees<br>Shaded by your light.<br>Please take me inside you, please take me in.<br>Never will I whisper, never will I give in.<br>Even when I'm dying, your heart will always win.<br>Shielded to the sightless, isolated from the naïve.<br>Breaking you in pieces, that can only ever grieve.<br>Veiled by your light.<br>Passionate for the world, yet overlooked by most.<br>Your soul flickers in you, desperate to shine for the world.<br>But blinded by your darkness.<br>Please take me inside you, please take me in. <br>Never will I whisper, never will I give in.<br>Even when I'm dying, your heart will always win."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>I really LOVED reading this story. I loved the strong personalities of both Ella and Micha and I loved the way the author Jessica Sorensen was able to give us a very clear perspective on both of the characters' point of view. Ella and Micha already have a special place in my heart and I can't wait to find out what the future holds in store for them so I'm definitely looking forward to the sequel <i>"The Forever of Ella and Micha"</i>!!! <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1350534855l/16055475.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes</u>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Just because it's broken, doesn't mean it loses its importance. And I figured I'd give it to you one day when you realized it was okay to make mistakes."<br><br>**<br><br>"I love you, Ella May and nothing will ever change that. You can push me away - run away - and I will still love you."<br><br>**<br><br>"When it all comes down to it, it's just me and her against the world. Always has been."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3513848921222573662" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer431678570" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13655414141787003333"><b> *** NEW COVER ALERT *** This book will be rereleased in March with this new cover.<br/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392726i/756056._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>4.5 stars<br/><br/><i> <b> “…when it all comes down to it, it’s just me and her against the world. Always has been.” </b></i> </b><br/><br/><b> A beautiful friends to lovers story about a girl from a broken home and the bad boy who made her feel loved and safe again. </b><br/><br/>Ella and Micha came from a life of broken homes and bad neighbourhoods but ever since childhood, they have been there for each other – the best of friends. As they grew up, Micha wanted more</span>
  <span id="freeText13655414141787003333" style="display:none"><b> *** NEW COVER ALERT *** This book will be rereleased in March with this new cover.<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392726i/756056._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>4.5 stars<br><br><i> <b> “…when it all comes down to it, it’s just me and her against the world. Always has been.” </b></i> </b><br><br><b> A beautiful friends to lovers story about a girl from a broken home and the bad boy who made her feel loved and safe again. </b><br><br>Ella and Micha came from a life of broken homes and bad neighbourhoods but ever since childhood, they have been there for each other – the best of friends. As they grew up, Micha wanted more but sensed something in Ella was holding her back and he never pushed her further.<br><br>Then one day, after their first kiss, Ella quite literally walks right out of his life. For eight months, he doesn’t hear a word from her. And ever since that day he has been desperately trying to find her.<br><br>Now, she suddenly she comes back home. But she has changed. Growing up, she always had been fiery – a rule breaker, an adreneline junkie, always speaking her mind, seizing the moment and taking risks – pretty much the girl equivalent of a bad boy. Now she’s a lot quieter, blends in more with people… is different.<br><br>But something made her leave and something is keeping her now from fully opening up to him and Micha will stop at nothing to figure out what has been keeping the girl he’s always been in love with away from him.<br><br><i> “See, the same old Ella still lives.” He grins… “She just needed a little push out.”…<br>“No, she doesn’t. She’s gone forever.”<br>“Try all you want, but I’m bringing her back,” </i><br><br>The characters are a wonderful mix of both endearing and mysterious. I felt like I knew just enough about them to connect me to them and to make me care but there was just enough that I didn’t know about them to keep up the mystery and the intrigue.<br><br>This book surprised me a lot – for some reason, this wasn’t the plot I was expecting but I really enjoyed the read.<br><br>Ella has pretty serious intimacy issues that stemmed from when she was a child – coming from a broken home, with a bi polar mother, a drunk father and an absentee brother… that kind of childhood would be bound to mark anyone.<br><br>But she had Micha who was just *swoon* a gorgeous character. A tattoed, musician bad boy with a lip ring, the kindest heart and a serious soft spot for this girl that he’s loved since he was sixteen.<br><br>It took Ella a while to accept Micha’s feelings for her. And at first I found it a little frustrating, but the more I learned about her character, the more I found her reactions understandable.<br><br>And when she finally realized that there’s this guy who has been there for her her whole life and whole is just head over heels in love with her – like truly, deeply in love – who’d do anything for her, oh my swoon is it beautiful!<br><br><i> <b> “I love you, Ella May and nothing will ever change that. You can push me away -run away – and I will still love you.” </b></i> <br><br>I could just feel how much he loved her. He’d do anything for her. Drop his life. Give up anything. This girl is his world. And he loved her enough to be patient with her and just be her friend while she sorted out her world.<br><br><i> “Stay here, baby,” he whispers…”Trust me, okay?” Don’t run.” </i><br><br>And guys, don’t go into this expecting some big “they-are-really-secret-agents” kind of secret. That’s really not the point of this book. The secrets are deeper than that. Its the complex sum of the emotions and experiences that have made them both who they are. What drives them. What kept them apart. What ultimately brings them together.<br><br>And omg the ending!! I swear my heart stopped! I was sensing a total <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15842441.Effortless__Thoughtless___2_" title="Effortless (Thoughtless, #2) by S.C. Stephens" rel="nofollow noopener">Effortless</a> vibe there. I totally didn’t expect that ending and I know everything will mostly likely be okay in the end but in the meantime, seriously… SNIFFFFFFF!!<br><br>Thank god for the mini-epilogue! It healed my heart and left me in a happy place…. but desperately looking forward to Book 2 “THE FOREVER OF ELLA AND MICHA” which will be released on November 3rd!! I WAN T MORE!!!<br><br>I definitely recommend giving this book a shot and guess what?? Its only $0.99 on Amazon right now so go go go !! <br><br>**little tidbit from the author: I was curious how to pronounce “Micha” whether it was Meesha or My-ka and she confirmed that the way she says it is “My-ka”<br><br>CASTING:<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379781721i/423061.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379781721i/423062.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="13655414141787003333" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_428017969" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/428017969" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/428017969?book_show_action=true">Oct 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Read w/my Smut Monday Girls, so them, haha</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Stacia (the 2010 club) by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/5744962-anna">Anna</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=new-adult-college">new-adult-college</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer428017969" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15732807265612448176"><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>The scream that shatters my mouth could shatter the world's happiness into a thousand pieces. But the silence that follows it is enough to dissolve it completely.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/>3.5 stars. With a review opener like that, you'd think I was about to delve right into talking about how crazy this book was, or how shocking the secret was. <br/><br/>Picture me doing that noise when you've hit a whammy...that wauh, wauh, wauh, noise. This book had a few secrets, but nothing really smacked me in the face. <br/><br/>However, I </span>
  <span id="freeText15732807265612448176" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>The scream that shatters my mouth could shatter the world's happiness into a thousand pieces. But the silence that follows it is enough to dissolve it completely.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br />3.5 stars. With a review opener like that, you'd think I was about to delve right into talking about how crazy this book was, or how shocking the secret was. <br /><br />Picture me doing that noise when you've hit a whammy...that wauh, wauh, wauh, noise. This book had a few secrets, but nothing really smacked me in the face. <br /><br />However, I did enjoy <i>Ella and Micha</i> It was a sweet and hot little friends-to-lovers story. Even though there was nothing new here and I felt like I'd read other, similar stories, I would recommend this book to anyone who enjoys watching the guy chase the girl as he's teasing her, plying her, and sexily begging her to give him a chance. These are the types of romances which get one's heart beating just a little bit faster. <br /><br />I would have preferred to have seen less cliches (constant references to eye color and smells, bad boy that's used everyone girl in his path while he only truly wants the one girl who's always evaded him, etc.), over-used romance terms (coming apart, ripples deep inside my core, etc.), and music references which will date the story in a few years - this was still a good effort for a first-in-a-series book. Something about this author's writing style reminds me of Abbi Glines - this could be either a good thing or a bad thing. While Glines is excellent at sexual tension, she tends to recycle her characters and plots too much for my liking. I'm honestly unsure why <i>Ella and Micha</i> wasn't a standalone book instead of a series, but since I was entertained by this couple, I'll go along for the ride and see where things take me.<br /><br />Overall, the steam factor was decent for a New Adult, and the romance was engaging. Since the book straddles the line in content between YA and Adult, I could see it appealing to readers of either medium. You can't go too wrong with a hot, up-and-coming rock star. Here's hoping that the drama ahead doesn't go too far into silly groupie stratosphere.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15732807265612448176" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText6676612658337272611" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>Ever wondered what would life be like if you could run away and be someone else? Go to a place where no one knows you and have a brand new beginning?? Who would you be then?? Ever thought about it??</i>

  <i>But is it really that easy to leave your past behind? Is it possible to be ever completely free from it?? To forget everything about it and those who were in it???</i>
</b><br><br>Meet <b>Ella May Daniels</b>, a girl who tried to run away from her past, who thought she could leave everything and everyone behind and become someone <b>in control of her fate</b>. She is a girl from the rougher side of the town....a girl who used to race with boys and against them, who spoke what was on her mind, who hung around with guys and acted like a <b>daredevil</b> and tried to show the world that she had a tough hide, who <b>didn't give a damn about what anybody else thought of her</b>.....and who <i>used to have studs on every item of clothing she owned and enough black eyeliner to make an entire sketch</i>...... ;)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399790i/774057.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But a night, one night changed all that.........<br><br><blockquote>

  </i>

  <i>unable to face herself in the mirror. Now secrets defined her.....</i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>A long time ago, it felt like home, back when street racing and running wild felt natural, but now I just feel lost.</b>
  </i>

  <i>
    <b>Shielded to the sightless, isolated from the naïve.<br>Breaking you in pieces, that can only ever grieve. <br>Veiled by your light. <br>Passionate for the world, yet overlooked by most. <br>Your soul flickers in you, desperate to shine for the world.<br>But blinded by your darkness. <br>Please take me inside you, please take me in. <br>Never will I whisper, never will I give in. <br>Even when I’m dying, your heart will always win.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399790i/774066._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>They have been together since the day he gave her his toy car and persuaded her to be his friend.....</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399790i/774067.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>They were together the day he cried and she gave him her Popsicle and sat with him till he ran out of tears...</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399790i/774068.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>But will they end up together forever??</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399790i/774069.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Read the book and find out..... ;)<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[It's not that big a secret....not something you won't come to know about in the beginning itself and the subject dealt with in this similar to that of the subject of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15990969.Ten_Tiny_Breaths" title="Ten Tiny Breaths by K.A. Tucker" rel="nofollow noopener">Ten Tiny Breaths</a> but the stories are very different...so if you're looking for a sweet and touching read, then this is the book for you!! :) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>-----------------------------------------------------------------------<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The lyrics used in this review is taken from the book itself in which Micha writes and sings this song for Ella. It's called 'What No One Ever Sees'. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Ella's feelings reminded me of this song by Demi Lovato......'Catch Me'....<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=SFEHOKdtdqo">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=SFEHOK...</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399790i/774070.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer438700611" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer9732424236856585259"><b>3 1/2 to 4 Stars </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412221884i/11342023._SX540_.png' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Overall, I enjoyed reading this book. The heroine's martyr-ism drove me crazy at time, but the awesomeness of the hero more than made up for it. Jessica Sorensen has a talent for <i>emo</i> storytelling that's as hopeful and sweet as it is depressing. There's a sequel but the "happy for now ending" left me more than satisfied. If you enjoy the new adult genre and don't mind an overabundance of angst and drama that surprisingly will also put a smile on your face while making you swoon, </span>
  <span id="freeText9732424236856585259" style="display:none"><b>3 1/2 to 4 Stars </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412221884i/11342023._SX540_.png" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall, I enjoyed reading this book. The heroine's martyr-ism drove me crazy at time, but the awesomeness of the hero more than made up for it. Jessica Sorensen has a talent for <i>emo</i> storytelling that's as hopeful and sweet as it is depressing. There's a sequel but the "happy for now ending" left me more than satisfied. If you enjoy the new adult genre and don't mind an overabundance of angst and drama that surprisingly will also put a smile on your face while making you swoon, then I definitely recommend this book. </span>

<div id="review_437511426" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/437511426" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/437511426?book_show_action=true">Oct 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=lost-love-rekindled">lost-love-rekindled</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=dark-angsty">dark-angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=shower-smexin">shower-smexin</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=tattooed-hero">tattooed-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer437511426" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4389720239359436061"><b>“I love you, Ella May and nothing will ever change that. You can push me away—run away—and I will still love you.”</b><br/><br/>This is such a sweet ‘new adult’ style romance between two friends, Ella and Micha, who have known each other forever, growing up together. They both come from dysfunctional families – Micha’s Dad ran out on them when he was 6 and Ella’s Dad is an alcoholic and her mother suffers from bipolar disorder with delusions of grandeur.<br/><br/>Just as Ella and Micha were about to take their relation</span>
  <span id="freeText4389720239359436061" style="display:none"><b>“I love you, Ella May and nothing will ever change that. You can push me away—run away—and I will still love you.”</b><br><br>This is such a sweet ‘new adult’ style romance between two friends, Ella and Micha, who have known each other forever, growing up together. They both come from dysfunctional families – Micha’s Dad ran out on them when he was 6 and Ella’s Dad is an alcoholic and her mother suffers from bipolar disorder with delusions of grandeur.<br><br>Just as Ella and Micha were about to take their relationship further than friendship one dark and stormy night, Ella decides to run to college without telling Micha where she is going. Traumas in her past that she blames herself for have pushed her over the edge and she decides to reinvent herself.<br><br>Now, 8 months later, she is back, barely recognisable as the girl that had run from Micha. The old Ella burned brightly with an inner fire, she was reckless and fiery and passionate and always honest. Now she has repressed all that we she was deep inside and created a façade of a polite and preppy student but Micah can still see the old Ella, his Ella, burning on the inside and he wants her back.<br><br>Ella broke my heart – her perceived guilt completely defines her. She’s pretending to be happy as the new Ella and not quite getting there, she’s not looking in mirrors because she can’t bear to look at herself, and she’s almost suffocating with panic over her memories. She’s been able to change who she is on the outside but can’t truly change what is on the inside and certainly can’t mask her body’s instinctive and fiery reaction to Micha and her blood is roaring with yearning to be close to him again. <br><br>Micha has his own demons to contend with but, despite growing up on the wrong side of the tracks, he’s incredibly mature and grounded and decides to hide these from Ella. He’s worried about her and instinctively wants to protect her. He’s confident he can rekindle the flame and bring the old Ella back.<br><br>They’re so sweet together – they complete each other. It’s a lovely young romance and I’m looking forward to the next chapter in their story.<br><br>Ella <br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394824i/760309.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Micha<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394824i/760310.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>My OCD needed to know how to pronounce Micha so I asked the author herself and she told me it is My-Kah.<br><br>4 stars new adult contemporary romance<br><br><i>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Blog</a></i></span>

<div id="review_539770799" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/539770799" />
    <a title="Mariella" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9860247-mariella"><img alt="Mariella" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/539770799?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mariella" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mariella" href="/user/show/9860247-mariella">Mariella</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer539770799" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3090455930911547244">I read this book because I loved "The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden", which was perfect to me. I liked the plot, I loved the heroine & her friend(s), and her love interest quickly became mine, too. Plus, the love scenes were incredibly sexy.<br/>But with this book, I was disappointed. The whole plot seemed ridicuous to me. I was always waiting for Ella to just stop stretching things out unneedlessly. And even though I knew that something terrible had happened to Ella in the past, it didn't make me</span>
  <span id="freeText3090455930911547244" style="display:none">I read this book because I loved "The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden", which was perfect to me. I liked the plot, I loved the heroine &amp; her friend(s), and her love interest quickly became mine, too. Plus, the love scenes were incredibly sexy.<br />But with this book, I was disappointed. The whole plot seemed ridicuous to me. I was always waiting for Ella to just stop stretching things out unneedlessly. And even though I knew that something terrible had happened to Ella in the past, it didn't make me sympathise with her. It was mentioned about three times in the whole book I guess, and I felt like the author was ticking it off a list, you know, like, "Okay, I need to tell the reader about her terrible past - check; etc.". It didn't feel real because it didn't really have any impact on the character, as it did with Callie and Kayden. And, I'm sorry, but I hated Ella's "best friend"(I have actually forgotten her name). She was really annoying with all her questions and being all naive and stuff, and the author's attempts (near the ending) to make her seem "flawed but lovely" only made it worse. That girl was just so unneccessary and ANNOYING, I can't even. There is no reason at all for her to part of this story, really!<br />Ella was always talking about how she changed and would never talk to Micha again, blabla, but she never showed any of that. I mean, the second time she runs into Micha, she just gives in. Yes, she does reject him from time to time, but very rarely and half-heartedly, too. The rejection never last long (minutes to hours). And it never seemed like she truly regretted any of the stuff she did with him (like kissing him, letting him touch her, etc).<br />Micha - he was quite annoying, too. Ella reminds me of Bella when she talks about Micha - if you know what I mean. And Micha himself - the author hands every single detail about Micha to the reader on a silver plate within the first few pages. He loves Ella, he wants to sleep with her and he likes cars. Seriously, his "flaw"(or whatever you want to call it) comes off exactly like the thing in Ella's past - like the author was ticking off points on a checklist. It's something that, in my own life, I would find horrible, but with Micha, I couldn't feel anything but boredom.<br />The whole story felt constructed - around a frame of (I admit it: quite hot) love scenes. It feels like the author just needed the story to put some space between those scenes, seriously.<br />Don't let me start about the ending. There is something with a car race near the end, and let me just say it, it's ridiculous and predictable. Neither that nor anything of the cheesy stuff afterwards made me interested in the sequel at all, so I am definitely not going to read it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3090455930911547244" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_430749941" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/430749941" />
    <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel"><img alt="♥Rachel♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363996055p2/5481477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/430749941?book_show_action=true">Oct 09, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Rachel♥" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel">♥Rachel♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer430749941" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7575425508674667702"><br/>The Secret of Ella and Micha was a romance full of <b>SMOKING</b> hot chemistry from years of pent up attraction. The best kind of romance, in my book, is one that starts from years of friendship and grows into so much more. *sigh*<br/><br/>After a night that scared her to the core, Ella Daniels picked up and left her hometown without a word to any of her friends. She doesn’t even tell her best friend, Micha, she just picks up and leaves. Ella has to return home after eight months hiding out at college, because </span>
  <span id="freeText7575425508674667702" style="display:none"><br />The Secret of Ella and Micha was a romance full of <b>SMOKING</b> hot chemistry from years of pent up attraction. The best kind of romance, in my book, is one that starts from years of friendship and grows into so much more. *sigh*<br /><br />After a night that scared her to the core, Ella Daniels picked up and left her hometown without a word to any of her friends. She doesn’t even tell her best friend, Micha, she just picks up and leaves. Ella has to return home after eight months hiding out at college, because she’s got no where else to go for the summer break. She dreads seeing Micha again because before she left, the tension that had been building between them led to an earth shattering kiss, and she doesn’t want to be tempted back into her old life again. What she doesn’t realize is how much she missed him and how good he is for her. Do you really have to change your whole personality to keep from repeating past mistakes? Ella’s about to find out. <br /><br />Micha was torn up the day Ella went missing. His whole focus was to find her. He stopped partying and playing music, and gave up girls too. Even though Ella and Micha weren’t a couple before she left, they we’re on that track. He was too afraid to admit his feelings to her for fear she’d bolt. Now that she’s back in town, Micha plans on showing Ella she can be herself without turning into her parents. He’s not going to let her run away from him this time! Luckily for Ella, Micha has a lot of patience and control. I love how he sticks it out for her and lays it all on the line:<br /><br /><b>
  <i>”I love you, Ella May and nothing will ever change that. You can push me away—run away—and I will still love you.”</i>
</b><br /><br />I love this type of romance where the characters have a history and know details about each other that only comes from time spent together. By the time Ella comes back, the feelings they have for each other have built up so much they’re about to explode! Here’s Ella’s thought when she first sees Micha again:<br /><br /><b>
  <i>If he keeps looking at me that way, my restraint is going to melt into a puddle of hot, steamy liquid. Micha has the most piercing eyes in the world, aqua blue, like the sea, waved with equal intensity. </i>
</b><br /><br />All I have to say is: “Give in Ella!” With those piercing blue eyes and his sexy lip ring, *dies* and a penchant for a little danger (muscle car street racing never sounded so hot!) who could blame a girl?! <br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7575425508674667702" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ari" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ari" href="/user/show/3564852-ari">Ari</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17370801-the-secret-of-ella-and-micha">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3564852-ari?shelf=annoyed-me">annoyed-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3564852-ari?shelf=n-a">n-a</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer587418764" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14028255203862168381"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417208i/824950.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>People should have real plots in their minds before starting to write a book. <br/>Seriously!<br/><br/>In fact they should read about 100 books in the same genre before coming up with a <i>new</i> story because they tend to do the same mistakes (and maybe they could learn from the others) and these stories tend to blend in with each other so that it would be funny if it weren't so annoying - really, there always seem to be two characters with broken lives (a tragedy in one's life is a must) that can't possibly be tog</span>
  <span id="freeText14028255203862168381" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417208i/824950.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>People should have real plots in their minds before starting to write a book. <br>Seriously!<br><br>In fact they should read about 100 books in the same genre before coming up with a <i>new</i> story because they tend to do the same mistakes (and maybe they could learn from the others) and these stories tend to blend in with each other so that it would be funny if it weren't so annoying - really, there always seem to be two characters with broken lives (a tragedy in one's life is a must) that can't possibly be together for no apparent reason (even though they like each other), but then all of the sudden they have sex and then simply makeup. <br>The end.<br><br>No, really, that's all there is to this story too. <br>Sounds familiar? <br>Well, maybe you've seen this in almost <i>all</i> the other books in this New Adult trend, huh? How'bout that? I bet it does ring a few bells.<br><br>I'm not sure about other readers, but I am getting really tired of this genre where all books have underdeveloped story-lines that get to nowhere, characters all over the place that think in a way and then act right the other way around (hello personality, nice to meat you but I don't need you in my book), awkward conversation that don't ever belong to real life... and I could still go on and on about the things I dislike about this NA thing, because they describe this story so 'nicely'. In fact I will mention one more thing: they are usually poorly written. <br><br>So this is me being done with this poor excuse of a genre, with this book that so many people liked that I'm starting to wonder if there's something wrong with <i>me</i> for not finding in the story all the things they raved about. <br>And no, don't get me wrong, I don't judge you if you liked this story, I am really glad for you... I just can't seem to find any kind of enjoyment in these books. That's all.<br><br>Happy midnight reading!<br>____________________________________________<br><br><a href="http://www.readingaftermidnight.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog (EN)</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/readingaftermidnight" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/lil_aree" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://readingaftermidnight.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> |<a href="http://www.bloglovin.com/en/blog/3285482/reading-after-midnight/" rel="nofollow noopener"> Bloglovin'</a> | <a href="http://ro.readingaftermidnight.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog (RO)</a><br>____________________________________________<br><br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer403499132" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18384001174783309631"><blockquote>
  <strong>
    <em>“There’s a darkness inside my chest, like the devil hidden inside me is about to make a grand appearance.”</em>
  </strong>
</blockquote><br/>This is the story of two young people, Micha and Ella, inseparable since childhood, daredevils at heart, ‘soul mates’ from the get go. One tragic event in Ella’s life changes everything - she loses herself in her pain, drowning in guilt and regret, and she does the only thing she can think of before her mind shatters completely - she runs away. She runs away from everything and e</span>
  <span id="freeText18384001174783309631" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <strong>
    <em>“There’s a darkness inside my chest, like the devil hidden inside me is about to make a grand appearance.”</em>
  </strong>
</blockquote><br />This is the story of two young people, Micha and Ella, inseparable since childhood, daredevils at heart, ‘soul mates’ from the get go. One tragic event in Ella’s life changes everything - she loses herself in her pain, drowning in guilt and regret, and she does the only thing she can think of before her mind shatters completely - she runs away. She runs away from everything and everyone she knows. She leaves the sad and guilt-ridden little girl behind to become a ‘new’ Ella that doesn't allow her emotions to rule her life. She can't fix the pain inside her chest but she can silence the screaming voice inside her head by re-inventing herself and regaining the control that she so desperately clings to. But Ella also ends up leaving behind the one person she loves the most in her life, the only person that knows even the deepest corners of her broken soul and loves her all the same - Micha.<br /><blockquote>
  <em>“Micha saw too much of me and it scared me too much to let him in all the way.”</em>
</blockquote><br />Micha is the proverbial bad boy - a road-racer, a musician, tattoos and piercing and all. But his tough guy appearance is just a façade. He is an incredibly sensitive and caring young man, a loyal friend, a responsible and loving son, a patient and selfless boyfriend. Micha and Ella’s friendship gradually blossoms into deep romantic feelings for each other, but while Micha embraces them wholeheartedly, Ella fights them with all she’s got, struggling to admit to herself that she is in love with her best friend.<br /><blockquote>
  <em>“I want Micha so bad it physically hurts sometimes. But if it hurts to want him this much, then how bad would it be to lose him?”</em>
</blockquote><br />Theirs is a story of friends becoming lovers, of allowing love into your heart even when feelings are the last thing you want to allow under your defensive cape. There is no way of fighting those feelings, especially ones that are so solidly founded on friendship and loyalty to each other. There is nothing Ella and Micha wouldn’t do for one another - they are each other’s anchor in a life that has been everything but kind to them.<br /><br />Once their friendship naturally evolves into romance, they tackle their relationship gently, never hastily or forcefully. They give each other time, space, support, they allow one another to find their footing and draw strength from their bond rather than let themselves be consumed by compulsion and chemistry. I particularly admired them for not just giving in to their desire to be together all the time, but instead continuing to pursue their own dreams as well, using their love as a source of courage and support, driving them forward and letting them take chances in their lives.<br /><br />By giving us alternating points of view, the author has made sure that we get to know both characters equally. We get to bond with each of them, loving them for such different reasons. We love Ella because she is a broken soul who is so scared of losing control and becoming like her mother that she was willing to give up on the greatest happiness that she had ever known in her life. We feel protective towards her, we want her safe, to shield her, … to give her Micha.<br /><blockquote> <em>“The kiss … was an earthshattering kiss, one that stole breaths, stopped hearts, and scared the sh*t out of me because it surfaced feelings I’d never felt before, ones that rendered me helpless.”</em></blockquote><br />Micha is an absolute dream. Ella is drawn to him because he is familiar, he is comforting, he gets her. He loves any and all versions of her, whether she decides to be a foul-mouthed eyeliner-wearing Goth, or a pastel-adoring cheerleader-type. His love for her left me gushing, sighing, drooling …<br /><blockquote>
  <em>“You can’t just change who you are in the outside and expect it to change who you are on the inside.”</em>
</blockquote><br />This is the story of a truly selfless love. Micha and Ella don’t suffocate each other with selfish demands, ultimatums or by manipulating each other’s feelings. Their friendship has made sure that they trust each other implicitly, always cheering each other on in everything they do. This book carries for me such a positive message amongst a myriad of similar stories where we are conditioned to equate over-possessiveness and jealousy with true affection, where mind-games are seen as endearing and where controlling one’s partner is considered sexy. I was drawn to the story from the very first page. These characters captured my heart, gave me a constant but gentle fluttering in my chest, making me feel what they were feeling and leaving me hungry for more of their story.<br /><p>The next book in The Secret series, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16055475.The_Forever_of_Ella_and_Micha__The_Secret___2_" title="The Forever of Ella and Micha (The Secret, #2) by Jessica Sorensen" rel="nofollow noopener">The Forever of Ella and Micha</a>, will be released on 3 November 2012, and the third book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16055479.The_Temptation_of_Lila_and_Ethan__The_Secret___3_" title="The Temptation of Lila and Ethan (The Secret, #3) by Jessica Sorensen" rel="nofollow noopener">The Temptation of Lila and Ethan</a>, on 29 December 2012. I. Cannot. Wait.<br /><br />~ N ♥<br /><br /><a href="http://wp.me/p2AtqW-wK" rel="nofollow noopener">See this review on my blog!</a> | <a href="http://www.facebook.com/natashaisabookjunkie" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow me on Facebook!</a><br /><br /></p></span>
  <a data-text-id="18384001174783309631" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2237788742137356849">I am baffled at how this book got such a high rating.<br/><br/>The writing was mediocre, at best... and, I'm sorry, but every time Micha "sucked on his lip ring" I got grossed out, which completely defeats the purpose of this book. The characters have no substance or personality, and every time Micha calls Ella "pretty girl" I just picture an obnoxious parrot screaming "Pretty girl, pretty girl."<br/><br/>It was a super quick and easy read, but I obviously won't be continuing with this series. </span>

<div id="review_447723895" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/447723895" />
    <a title="Sandra " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9752625-sandra"><img alt="Sandra " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345749155p2/9752625.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/447723895?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sandra " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sandra " href="/user/show/9752625-sandra">Sandra </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=omfg">omfg</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=liked-the-characters-some-or-all">liked-the-characters-some-or-all</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=need-a-change-of-panties">need-a-change-of-panties</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=sad">sad</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=sexy-males">sexy-males</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=rolling-my-eyes">rolling-my-eyes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=don-t-like-the-main-character">don-t-like-the-main-character</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=horrible-bad-boring-beginnings">horrible-bad-boring-beginnings</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=melting-inside-awwww">melting-inside-awwww</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=panic-attack">panic-attack</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer447723895" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15734878514513439239"><blockquote>
  <b>"Micha, this is who I have to be otherwise I can't breathe. Please just leave it alone. That dame fire might exist, but I want it gone." I spin my back to him, praying he'll listen to me for once, because if he keeps it up, sooner or later I won't be able to resist. But Micha has never backed down on a challenge in his life."<br/></b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><i>The Secret of Ella and Micha</i> was a <b>beautiful</b> and <b>touching </b>read about <b>forgiveness</b>, <b>moving on</b>, and <b>love</b>. About a girl who lost herself on the way of grief and blame, and a</span>
  <span id="freeText15734878514513439239" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>"Micha, this is who I have to be otherwise I can't breathe. Please just leave it alone. That dame fire might exist, but I want it gone." I spin my back to him, praying he'll listen to me for once, because if he keeps it up, sooner or later I won't be able to resist. But Micha has never backed down on a challenge in his life."<br></b>
</blockquote><br><br><i>The Secret of Ella and Micha</i> was a <b>beautiful</b> and <b>touching </b>read about <b>forgiveness</b>, <b>moving on</b>, and <b>love</b>. About a girl who lost herself on the way of grief and blame, and a boy who was trying to put her back together, even if he was broken himself. He was trying to destroy the walls she has put around herself.<br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396390i/764034._SY540_.jpg" alt="20b796a3 1d0d 4c4f bbea b00d1d35470d zps179d65b5" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>The girl he thought he loved needs to disappear. I don't want tonight to be irreversible, so i pull away, breathing him in one last time.</b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>When Ella went away to collage she left everything behind. <br>And turned into someone else, hiding her pain behind a mask she put on. <br>But now it's summer, and she has nowhere else to go.<br>Except back to Micha...<br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396390i/764035.jpg" alt="a9500ff6 3699 42d4 a7c7 3582cdf405de zpsaab2a498" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br>Micha can get under Ella's skin like no one else<br>He'll temp the old Ella back at any costs. <br>And she knows it'll be hard to resist.<br>Will her facade break?<br><br>Will the secret of Ella and Micha be revealed? </b><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396390ra/764036.gif" alt="tumblr mlxtja ZJqc1qjtku3o1 500 zps5cf1935f" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br>For some reason i couldn't get into this book in the beginning at all. Maybe because Ella was annoying me. She is one of those characters that deny love because of something that isn't their fault, and for a stupid reason in general. They keep on thinking they don't deserve anything, as a result push people away, and that get's on my nerves pretty badly. <br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396390ra/764037.gif" alt="stash 1 50ecaab44da9e zpsd157500e" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>When it all comes down to it, it's just me and her against the world. Always has been.</b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>I loved Micha!</b> He's not only a solo guitarist with an amazing, and sexy voice. But he's also a real hottie who takes care of Ella, supports her, helps her, and is always there for her even when she wasn't there for him. Even when she pushes him away he stands his ground and tries to turn her back into a girl she once was. <br><br> <a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396390ra/764038.gif" alt="tumblr lylefh3ox U1qep71v" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br>And there is definitely something more to Ella's friend - Lila. She seemed cliche to the readers, even to the characters from the book. But i <b>feel</b> like there is something more hidden down there, and i would love it if she got her own book or trilogy/series.<br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396390ra/764039.gif" alt="tumblr mnqs0ngl En1srauo2o1 500" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br>What was the most beautiful thing about this book was the relationship between Ella and Micha. There were so many hot and sweet scenes between them, like; When they made out in the shower, or when he climbed though her window and fell asleep next to her.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"As carefully as I can, I step over her bed and crawl in with Ella. I press my chest against her back, drape my arm over her waist, and feel the rhythm of her breathing. God, I've missed this way too much. It's not healthy. I burrow my face in her neck, smelling the scent of her hair, vanilla mixed with something that's only her. <br>I shut my eyes and for the first time in eight months, I fall into a peaceful sleep."</b>
</blockquote><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396390ra/764040.gif" alt="awww eccbc87e4b5ce2fe28308fd9f2a7baf3 169" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br>I had a little panic attack towards the end. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[When the car wrecked with Micha and Ethan when they were racing (even though it was predictable something bad was about to happen.) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> However, i'm glad they made it and everyone was happy.<br><br>Overall, <i>The Secret of Ella and Micha</i> was a wonderful read that had me swooning and touched my heart. Really great read about childhood best friends to lovers kinda thing. Definitely recommend this, and i'll be reading book 2 for sure soon! I'll leave you off with one of Micha's songs for Ella...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>" I see it in your beautiful eyes, like a spot on the sun.<br>The things you want to hide, buried deep inside you.<br>Blinded by your light.<br>It almost hurts to look at, almost hurts to breathe.<br>Never can you look at the things no one ever sees<br>Shaded by your light.<br>Please take me inside you, please take me in.<br>Never will I whisper, never will I give in.<br>Even when I'm dying, your heart will always win.<br>Shielded to the sightless, isolated from the naïve.<br>Breaking you in pieces, that can only ever grieve.<br>Veiled by your light.<br>Passionate for the world, yet overlooked by most.<br>Your soul flickers in you, desperate to shine for the world.<br>But blinded by your darkness.<br>Please take me inside you, please take me in. <br>Never will I whisper, never will I give in.<br>Even when I'm dying, your heart will always win."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
