<div id="review_413894914" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/413894914" />
    <a title="Annie Brewer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5315988-annie-brewer"><img alt="Annie Brewer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442496062p2/5315988.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/413894914?book_show_action=true">Sep 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie Brewer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie Brewer" href="/user/show/5315988-annie-brewer">Annie Brewer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer413894914" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13710599597404262059">Awwwwwwwwww that was beautiful. The ending was perfect....and I just loved this book so much!!!! Ella, Micha, Lila and Ethan were all great characters. I can not wait to continue with the next book!!! It truly had my heart soaring with joy, love and a lot of heart pounding....holy crap-the sexual tension was Hot hot hot!!!!!! <br/><br/>"Suddenly, I get a little nervous. This is the first time I've ever been with someone I've cared about and it's going to be different." -Micha<br/><br/><br/>First of all, I love that cove</span>
  <span id="freeText13710599597404262059" style="display:none">Awwwwwwwwww that was beautiful. The ending was perfect....and I just loved this book so much!!!! Ella, Micha, Lila and Ethan were all great characters. I can not wait to continue with the next book!!! It truly had my heart soaring with joy, love and a lot of heart pounding....holy crap-the sexual tension was Hot hot hot!!!!!! <br /><br />"Suddenly, I get a little nervous. This is the first time I've ever been with someone I've cared about and it's going to be different." -Micha<br /><br /><br />First of all, I love that cover. Wow, just the cover makes me swoon! And I never really found lip piercings to be that sexy-but Micha changes my mind completely. So aside from the cover-which is screaming to be read, I found myself really enjoying this ride.<br /><br />Ella and Micha were best friends for a very long time. They went through so much together. But one night-8 months ago, Ella up and leaves. Leaving her past-and Micha behind to attend college in Las Vegas without so much as a goodbye. Ella is trying to reinvent herself, she was not happy with who she was and tries to go for the good girl persona instead of the "I don't take shit from anyone" attitude that makes her so darn irresistable to Micha. That version was also the one that made him fall in love her. But when she comes back for the summer having nowhere else to, she is forced to relive her past where her mother killed herself, her dad is an alcohlic and estranged brother gets engaged without telling anyone since he lives away from home and loses contact with the family. It's also where she has to confront her feelings for Micha once and for all.<br /><br />Micha is your amazing tongue pierced, sexy bad boy who spent the last 8 months searching for the one that got away. He's loved her for years and the night he tells her is the night she leaves him. He's heartbroken and miserable without his best friend. Determined to find her when she shows up at home-next door I might add. When he meets the new Ella-he's not pleased. He wants his old Ella back-the one that made his body do crazy things. The one that screamed sexy things in his mind and lose himself in her. He meets Ella's college roommate Lila, which both of them know 2 very different versions of the same person. Can he bring back the old Ella without destroying her? <br /><br /><br />I loved this book-to pieces. It was really a beautiful story of friendship, love, pain, grief, loss and healing. Both characters are dealing with pasts that haunt them. But together, they are stronger people than they realize and in order to face their demons, they have to come face to face with their feelings for each other.<br /><br />I didn't cry with this book. But it was emotional at times. However, every scene with Micha made my body do crazy things. He was just amazing and sexy and very swoony. <br /><br /><br />“when it all comes down to it, it’s just me and her against the world. Always has been.”-Micha<br /><br />I loved reading this book from Micha's POV. His voice was sweet yet entrancing. I really felt his pain when he felt he lost his best friend. Or when he was going through that brief encounter with his dad. My heart ached for him. But he was a tough guy and eventhough you could tell through his facade, he was also an emotional sweet guy. I loved that he wasn't completely macho. It's always nice to see emotions peek through when it comes to guys. But every chapter with his voice I was giddy. I can never say enough-I'M A SUCKER FOR THE MALE'S POV!! And his did not disappoint. I heart you Micha Scott! *swoon*<br /><br />Ella was a great character. She was not annoying and once her resolve broke and crumpled to the ground-I liked her even more. I know she had been through alot and was scared about her feelings for Micha, but it was obvious how much she loved him. It pissed me off though when she would tell him she didn't want him with any other girl yet she wouldn't tell him why. I wanted to hit her. But once her words were out there, I felt better and less inclined to smack a bitch up, which was good though because I really liked Ella.<br /><br />I loved Ethan and Lila. Both were great secondary characters. Although in the beginning, I was skeptical of Lila. She seemed too prim and proper and I was wondering how she would really fit in with Ella's life. But eventually she warmed up to me and I even feel like there is more to her than meets the eye. I liked her and Ethan's chemistry. There seems to be something there and I can't wait to read the third book in this trilogy-which is Ethan and Lila's story. YAY!!!!<br /><br />Overall, this was a wonderful read through and through. I was glad I picked it up. It did not disappoint-which makes me happy because holy bloody fucking hell, that cover is GORGEOUS!!!!! So go get this book and read it. It's really worth the read! Also, it's a little quicker than I would have liked so hopefully the sequel is longer because I want more Ella and Micha. And definitely want more steam because their sexual tension is UHHHH-MAZING!!!!! I seriously wanted a cold shower after a few scenes. Sheeeesh! LOVE!!! <br /><br />Amazing 5 star read! <br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13710599597404262059" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_617604485" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/617604485" />
    <a title="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library"><img alt="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1350750103p2/4551536.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/617604485?book_show_action=true">May 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" href="/user/show/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library">Maja (The Nocturnal Library)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17370801-the-secret-of-ella-and-micha">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=contemporary-fiction">contemporary-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=failed-to-impress">failed-to-impress</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=review-copy">review-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=own-a-dtb">own-a-dtb</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=reviewed-in-2013">reviewed-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer617604485" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6753619596552125192">To repeat what I tweeted while I was halfway through this book – All this angst and not a single blueberry muffin in sight! Life can be so unfair sometimes. <br/><br/>Honestly, this book oozes angst, and while I know there are many readers who enjoy just that (proven by the very fact that this book is a New York Times bestseller), I’m not a fan myself. However, that’s not to say that I didn’t enjoy this book – I did. I just thought it was pushed a bit too far at times. <br/><br/>Ella and Micha have been best friend</span>
  <span id="freeText6753619596552125192" style="display:none">To repeat what I tweeted while I was halfway through this book – All this angst and not a single blueberry muffin in sight! Life can be so unfair sometimes. <br><br>Honestly, this book oozes angst, and while I know there are many readers who enjoy just that (proven by the very fact that this book is a New York Times bestseller), I’m not a fan myself. However, that’s not to say that I didn’t enjoy this book – I did. I just thought it was pushed a bit too far at times. <br><br>Ella and Micha have been best friends since childhood, but they were always either too afraid to take their friendship further, or there was something standing in their way. Neither of them comes from a happy home. Ella’s mother is dead and her father is an alcoholic, and Micha’s father walked out ages ago, never to be heard from again. Through it all, they always had each other, until one day, Ella just packed up and disappeared, without telling anyone where she can be found.<br><br>Micha spent the next eight months obsessively searching for Ella. He always knew he loved her, but he waited for her to come to him, and when she left, he realized it might be too late. He put his life on hold and moved heaven and earth to find her, but Ella was nowhere to be found. When she suddenly reappeared, Micha decided he’d waited long enough. It was clear to him that he and Ella were made for each other, so all he had to do was convince her of that fact. <br><br>In a way, I’m glad neither Ella nor Micha resolved their family situations in the end. That would have turned this book into a fairy tale, and I dislike fairy tales on principle. It was never about making their lives perfect, it was about facing everything that comes at them together. Things as big as alcoholism or estrangement can’t be resolved overnight, but I loved seeing them make their peace with their respective situations. <br><br>Although I’m not in the habit of punishing books (or authors) for things that are entirely the publisher’s fault, I feel I have to point out that The Secret of Ella and Micha is chock full of editing issues. There are spelling errors, grammar errors and formatting errors on almost every page. I realize it was self-published first, but I thought the whole purpose of traditional publishing was to avoid this kind of thing. A half-decent copy editor could have fixed this in no more than a few days. <br><br>Clearly every successful book gives birth to a trilogy these days, and that is the case with The Secrets of Ella and Micha. They will be getting a sequel soon that will apparently focus on their family situations and issues with long distance relationship. After that, Lila and Ethan will be getting their own book as well. <br><br><a href="http://www.thenocturnallibrary.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380226536i/681142.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>

<div id="review_413937132" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/413937132" />
    <a title="Erin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4979538-erin"><img alt="Erin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1520654483p2/4979538.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/413937132?book_show_action=true">Sep 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Erin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Erin" href="/user/show/4979538-erin">Erin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of Pushing the Limits</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4979538-erin?shelf=romance-erotica-faves">romance-erotica-faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4979538-erin?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer413937132" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11287977648648275805">WOW!! Holy hot tension with a smokin' bad boy!! I dove into this story the night it started popping up on GR, and my heart is still racing from the chemistry between these characters!! Secret is a heart-wrenching, captivating, sexy thrill ride of a romance story that grips you to the last page, and I just LOVED it!<br/><br/>First of I am head-over-heels for Micah!!! He embodied all of my favorite bad-boy qualities, being the gorgeous trouble-making daredevil with the heart of gold and mind in the gutter!!</span>
  <span id="freeText11287977648648275805" style="display:none">WOW!! Holy hot tension with a smokin' bad boy!! I dove into this story the night it started popping up on GR, and my heart is still racing from the chemistry between these characters!! Secret is a heart-wrenching, captivating, sexy thrill ride of a romance story that grips you to the last page, and I just LOVED it!<br /><br />First of I am head-over-heels for Micah!!! He embodied all of my favorite bad-boy qualities, being the gorgeous trouble-making daredevil with the heart of gold and mind in the gutter!! We get to see both his and Ella's POV, and honestly I was looking forward to every chapter from his filthy mind! *swoons* But he was so incredibly gone for Ella, having spent the 8 months since she picked up and left him desperately trying to find her so he could feel whole again. She was his heart, and when she left he just wasn't the same, and the moment she steps back into his life it was like a meteor landing at his feet! He needs her more than she could ever imagine, and I was just melting over the love he has for her! Ella, having changed her whole persona to forget about her miserable life back home, was a bit snotty at first. She was so intent on denying her roots and her messed up childhood that she threw away everything and everyone to be this new person. But Micah slowly starts to pull the real Ella out-not necessarily the same reckless, immature girl that left town, but certainly not the stuck-up student that came home for the summer!<br /><br />The more Ella tries to deny her feelings for Micah, the more he pushes her to admit they were meant for each other. She pretends to think it's just Micah being Micah, but deep down she knows what he feels for her. Which scares her to death. Her life with a bi-polar mother who took her own life, and a father who's turned into a useless drunk, makes her put up giant walls around her heart. But being back at home, back around Micah and their old lives, makes her realize she can't just hide away, and there was SO much anticipation and tension as Micah whittled away at her defenses!!! It was HOT, HOT, HOT!! There aren't a lot of characters with chemistry together that's good enough to make my heart race over a kiss alone, but DANG, Sorensen had me breathless over these two just from the makeout sessions (and there were several)!! And I really loved that they didn't just jump into bed together, too, it would have cheapened the moment. It was well worth the wait, believe me!! <br /><br />I didn't realize going into this that there was a second book, so I'm REALLY excited for more of these characters! Their story still has much to be told, and I can't wait to see Micah and Ella finally get their HEA!! </span>
  <a data-text-id="11287977648648275805" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Please just leave it alone. That damn fire might exist, but i want it gone." <br />Favorite Character - Elle<br /><br /><b>They don't know my head is a mess<br />No, they don't know who I really am<br />And they don't know what <br />I've been through like you do<br />And I was made for you...</b><br /><br />Oh god i <u>LOVED</u> this book. <br />It was heartbreaking at times reading how Elle felt, so truly moving. Elle was such a brilliantly complex character who i couldn't help but love as soon as i was introduced to her. I felt consumed by Elle &amp; Micha's emotions. Their chemistry was sublime, the build up of sexual tension was delicious. The affection which either lead had for each other was beautiful. They were each others band-aid's. I got lost in the story, I never wanted it to end. <br /><br />I would recommend this book &amp; I cannot wait to read the next in the series. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7755307115218487790" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

She was determined to show everyone that she was the “new” Ella. <br>But Micha was not convinced.<br>He wants her Ella back and he was going to do everything he can to make sure it happens.</i><br><br><b>FIRST IMPRESSIONS</b><br><br>I have always been a sucker for pretty covers. This one definitely has to be one of them. I mean just look at the two of them. Don’t they just look cute? The girl with the fiery red lipstick and the hot guy with the lip ring wanting to kiss each other but don’t want to because they were trying to be cute? Hahaha. But they are cute. And I think they were a good representation of the book. The cover was not deceiving because the inside of the book was just as cute as the cover.<br><br><b>CHARACTERS</b><br><br><b>Ella</b><br><br>I liked the before Ella really. I mean all of us mistakes and it was only right that she gets the chance to forgive herself for those. Although the old Ella was a little wild and carefree and sometimes out of control, I liked her because she was true to herself. I have never been a fan of people who try to change who they are because they always think of how other people will think of them. Ella was a sad, broken girl felt that she didn’t have anything in her life. She had a mother who was bipolar, a father who drunk himself to death and a brother who was the first to leave the house because he doesn’t want to deal with all of it. Who could blame Ella for wanting to make a change in her life to improve herself? I definitely don’t but leaving your problems behind and pretending it isn’t there doesn’t solve anything. But Ella was a strong girl. I admired her will for a change but I have to admit I got pretty pissed that she was trying to push away the person who cared the most about her. Who? Well you should know that by now already. :p<br><br><b>Micha</b><br><br>And then we have Micha, the not-so-knight-in-shining-armor of our story. Why did I say that? Because Prince Charming is supposed to be all perfect, who has everything planned out for himself and his future princess. But Micha wasn’t that. He was hot as hell sure plus he definitely knows how to <s>please a woman!!!</s> take care of the people he loves but still he wasn’t perfect. Micha was Ella’s knight in shining armor but he was rough around the edges which I think was even better. Micha’s character was totally believable. I love him because he wasn’t perfect. He has his flaws too especially when it comes to his father <s>who I’d rather not talk about</s>. Another thing I’d like to emphasize, Micha is just HOT AS HELL with all that singing of his with a ring on his lip. Not only that he also has, additional things that he could do that I’d rather not mention because just thinking about it makes me… <s>aroused</s> <s>heated up</s> HAPPY. Yeah reading about Micha makes me happy. :p<br><br>*There were bunch of other characters in the story but I’d like to focus on the two because mainly the story revolves around them. I’d like to still introduce you guys to Lila and Ethan. I liked those two because they were good friends to our lovely couple. Lila was your typical rich kid but then again after reading about her, I kind of liked her even though she was still a rich spoiled brat to me. Ethan also has his story to tell I believe but I guess that is for another story. Oh did I totally forgot the part that I think Lila and Ethan have a thing for each other? :p<br><br><b>MICHA + ELLA = JAM-PACKED WITH SEXUAL TENSION</b><br><br>I love Micha and Ella to death but as I was reading this book I wanted to smack Ella in the head the whole time. I wanted to shake her up and say, “GIRL YOU ARE PASSING UP AN AWESOME GUY! WAKE UP!” Good of her to listen though. :p Anyhow, I knew these two liked each other way before they admitted it to each other. I don’t know how it is with long-term friends being lovers but I am sure it’s a little awkward. Maybe that could be one of the reasons why all those sexual tension build up as high as the Eiffel Tower. I mean GAAAWWWD Ella, were you really going to say no to Micha? <s> I sure hell wouldn’t.</s> <br><br>Also be ready for a lot of this:<br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/kissing%20gif/jamieshaylanliu/12345.gif?o=22" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380333950ra/693548.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And this:<br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/kissing%20gif/cheesegirl33/GIF/GIF%20Battlestar%20Galactica/kissing.gif?o=110" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398894ra/771328.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><b>QUOTABLE QUOTES</b><br><br><i>“I love you, Ella May and nothing will ever change that. You can push me away -run away – and I will still love you.”<br><br>“You've always had a good grasp on what's right and wrong. You just have a hard time admitting that sometimes you choose the wrong.”<br><br>“Before I took off, the boundaries of our friendship were starting to blur. I thought time would fix this, but it seems like we’re back to where we started. As much as I would love to melt into him, it just can’t happen. I can’t open up like that and lose control. I need control.”<br><br>“Something snaps inside me, like a rubber band. With one swift movement, and the aid of my own willingness, Micha lifts me over the console and I straddle his lap, looping my arms around his neck.”<br><br>“We don’t speak as we stare up at the sky. He traces his finger along the folds between my fingers and my eyelids drifts shut. I feel a wall crumble, leaving behind dust, debris and pieces that desperately need to be put back together.”</i><br><br><b>HIGHLIGHTS</b><br><br>* The alternating Point-of-Views between Ella and Micha made this book. I think it wouldn’t be as effective if we were just reading the story in Ella’s POV. I wouldn’t have enjoyed it as much if it was. Because for a story like this to work, you’ll have to know what both party are thinking while the situations happen just like with this book.<br><br>* The story was simple and easy to follow. There were no deep plotline but I appreciated it just the way it was because for me it felt more character driven which worked. I felt more connected to the story because I knew where the story was going so what I really was looking out for was the reaction of the characters to the situations that they were facing.<br><br>* The characters were believable. There was no extraordinary stuff going on like the male lead character was the perfect one and tried to make the girl see that she was too. No, there was no crap like that. What we see here, are two emotionally driven characters who were flawed and in need of love that they eventually found with each other. Simple yes, but the process of these two characters getting there was a long and tedious one. Like I said, the story was simple but the characters were not so which I think made it all work.<br><br><b>FINAL WORDS</b><br><br>What can I say? I was totally blown away by this book. It was definitely not what I was expecting it to be. There were a mix of emotion here and there with a wide array of witty lines that made me smile and sometimes frown <s>I sometimes hate Ella’s negativism</s>. <br><br>If you are looking for a love story that will make your head hurt because of all the complexities then I don’t suggest you reading this.<br>This book was simple and genuine. Like I said, there was nothing bewildering about the story. There was nothing that would make you jump out of your seats because it scared or surprised the shit out of you. No there’s nothing like that here. <s>Unless you count the steamy scenes between them there are loads of that in this book</s> What you will have though is a glimpse of how two people who someone lost each other and found their way back and how they did it.<br><br>I am honestly happy that I picked up this book and read about Ella and Micha. I have never really understood how friendship and love works because it never happened to me. I have always believed that the best relationship starts with strangers but these two made me realize how important friendship is to make things work out. They weren’t sure where to start but eventually they found their way. <br><br>Would I recommend it? HELL YEAH! <br>Just a warning though, this book has a lot of sexual situations and mature contents like gif here below:<br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/kissing%20gif/dc20121/Just%20Another%20Day/MaitePerroniKissingandSex.gif?o=116" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398894ra/771329.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>so if you’re not ready to read something like that please don’t pick this book up because it is full of it. Although I would have to emphasize, THIS WAS AN AWESOME READ!<br><br><br>*************************************<br>PRE-REVIEW:<br><br><br>Geeezzlleeeewiiiizzzz! :)<br>I finished it last night because I couldn't put it off for another day.<br>There was just so much sexual tension it made me want to do sommersaults in a wire like this guy below.<br><br><a href="http://www.gifbin.com/983823" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398894ra/771330.gif" alt="funny gifs" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Micha is just so freakin' hot!<br>My imagination went into overdrive as I was reading it. :p<br><br><s>Micha! Come on here so we could make sweet love! </s><br><br><a href="http://www.gifbin.com/981926" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398894ra/771331.gif" alt="funny gifs" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Review to follow. :)</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2141788911?book_show_action=true">Oct 05, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elle&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elle&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/44344367-elle-s-book-blog">Elle&#39;s Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17371243-the-secret-of-ella-and-micha">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44344367-elle-s-book-blog?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44344367-elle-s-book-blog?shelf=college-romance">college-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2141788911" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5994793772440422949"><b> Release Date: </b> February 12, 2013<br/><b> Genre: </b> New Adult Romance<br/><br/>I have had this book sitting on my kindle since it was published and haven't gotten around to reading it until now. For the most part, I thought this was a nice new adult romance. It's a friends to lovers that spans many years in the making. Both characters- Ella and Micha- have some flaws though and things from their past that continue to haunt them in the present so the build up to the romance is pretty angsty. It takes them a while to</span>
  <span id="freeText5994793772440422949" style="display:none"><b> Release Date: </b> February 12, 2013<br /><b> Genre: </b> New Adult Romance<br /><br />I have had this book sitting on my kindle since it was published and haven't gotten around to reading it until now. For the most part, I thought this was a nice new adult romance. It's a friends to lovers that spans many years in the making. Both characters- Ella and Micha- have some flaws though and things from their past that continue to haunt them in the present so the build up to the romance is pretty angsty. It takes them a while to get close especially considering one left for 8 months without a word to the other, but when they finally do there are certainly fireworks. In some instances I had a hard time connecting with the characters- both of them actually. I think they were really closed off which in turn can hurt a story if readers like me aren't able to connect with them on a deep level. However, because there is a second book I gave it 4 stars. I am hoping that they open up a bit more and grow in the next one which I do plan to read. <br /><br />If you like new adult romances, this is one of the popular ones that many readers rave about so I would recommend it. I can see why people love it so much. <br /><br /><b>Perfect for Fans of </b><br />- New Adult Romance<br />- College Romance<br />- Friends to Lovers Romance<br />- Angsty Romances<br />- Romances that have characters with flaws and issues dealing with their pasts. </span>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('amaaUXmjCnlouBU1MLe95KWpbErO0/CYJP4UWxBtWlOIcnPGc2NAeqUbqgCm5BvAr0iLRuZVehTL77/kQq2o9w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Wx8G1Fso3BqTyMI9iHXlEnQBQIWQcSIbrrDSqh8JnTW5C+9DUeiWGV5rfQgeJkM2fuCnibj3qJdBoXkVTclvkQ==')})
  }
